### [176] [Talk Freely, Execute Strictly: Schema-Gated Agentic AI for Flexible and Reproducible Scientific Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06394)
*Joel Strickland,Arjun Vijeta,Chris Moores,Oliwia Bodek,Bogdan Nenchev,Thomas Whitehead,Charles Phillips,Karl Tassenberg,Gareth Conduit,Ben Pellegrini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出schema-gated orchestration架构，通过模式验证作为执行边界，解决LLM驱动的科学工作流中确定性执行与对话灵活性之间的权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型可以将自然语言目标转化为可执行计算，但科学工作流需要确定性、可追溯性和治理保障，而LLM自主决策难以满足这些要求。研究发现工业研发中存在两个竞争需求：确定性约束执行与不僵化的对话灵活性。

Method: 提出schema-gated orchestration作为解决方案，将模式作为组合工作流级别的强制执行边界。将需求操作化为执行确定性(ED)和对话灵活性(CF)，使用多模型协议评估20个系统，通过3个LLM家族的15个独立会话进行评分。

Result: 多模型LLM评分显示出高度一致性（ED的α=0.80，CF的α=0.98），可作为人类专家评估的替代方案。分析发现经验帕累托前沿，没有系统同时实现高灵活性和高确定性，但在生成式和流程中心极端之间存在收敛区域。

Conclusion: schema-gated架构通过分离对话和执行权限，能够解耦这一权衡。提炼出三个操作原则：执行前澄清、约束性计划-执行编排、工具到工作流级别的门控，以指导实际应用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can now translate a researcher's plain-language goal into executable computation, yet scientific workflows demand determinism, provenance, and governance that are difficult to guarantee when an LLM decides what runs. Semi-structured interviews with 18 experts across 10 industrial R&D stakeholders surface 2 competing requirements--deterministic, constrained execution and conversational flexibility without workflow rigidity--together with boundary properties (human-in-the-loop control and transparency) that any resolution must satisfy. We propose schema-gated orchestration as the resolving principle: the schema becomes a mandatory execution boundary at the composed-workflow level, so that nothing runs unless the complete action--including cross-step dependencies--validates against a machine-checkable specification.
  We operationalize the 2 requirements as execution determinism (ED) and conversational flexibility (CF), and use these axes to review 20 systems spanning 5 architectural groups along a validation-scope spectrum. Scores are assigned via a multi-model protocol--15 independent sessions across 3 LLM families--yielding substantial-to-near-perfect inter-model agreement (Krippendorff a=0.80 for ED and a=0.98 for CF), demonstrating that multi-model LLM scoring can serve as a reusable alternative to human expert panels for architectural assessment.
  The resulting landscape reveals an empirical Pareto front--no reviewed system achieves both high flexibility and high determinism--but a convergence zone emerges between the generative and workflow-centric extremes. We argue that a schema-gated architecture, separating conversational from execution authority, is positioned to decouple this trade-off, and distill 3 operational principles--clarification-before-execution, constrained plan-act orchestration, and tool-to-workflow-level gating--to guide adoption.

</details>

### [177] [Omni-C: Compressing Heterogeneous Modalities into a Single Dense Encoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05528)
*Kin Wai Lau,Yasar Abbas Ur Rehman,Lai-Man Po,Pedro Porto Buarque de Gusmão*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: Omni-C是一个统一的密集Transformer编码器，通过单模态对比预训练学习跨图像、音频和文本的共享表示，无需MoE架构或配对监督，显著降低推理内存使用


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态系统依赖独立专家编码器导致计算复杂度线性增长，而统一Omni模型虽然使用MoE架构但仍增加参数量和路由开销，需要更高效的多模态学习方案

Method: 提出Omni-C单密集Transformer编码器，通过大规模未对齐数据的单模态对比预训练学习共享表示，使用轻量级模态特定投影头，支持顺序模态处理和低内存推理

Result: 在单模态和跨模态任务上达到与专家模型相当的性能，音频和文本的零样本性能有轻微下降但可通过轻量级线性探测或参数高效微调恢复，相比多编码器基线显著降低推理内存使用

Conclusion: Omni-C通过统一的密集架构和参数共享，在不使用MoE、配对监督或路由的情况下实现了高效可扩展的多模态学习，为内存受限系统提供了实用的解决方案

Abstract: Recent multimodal systems often rely on separate expert modality encoders which cause linearly scaling complexity and computational overhead with added modalities. While unified Omni-models address this via Mixture-of-Expert (MoE) architectures with specialized experts and routing, they still inflate parameter counts and introduce routing overhead. In this paper, we propose Omni-C (Omni-Compress), a single dense Transformer-based encoder that learns competitive shared representations across heterogeneous modalities--images, audio, and text--through unimodal contrastive pretraining on large-scale unaligned data. By maximizing parameter sharing in the backbone and using lightweight modality-specific projection heads, Omni-C effectively mitigates inter-modality conflicts without requiring MoE, paired supervision, or routing. This design supports efficient deployment on memory-constrained systems via sequential modality processing and low-memory inference, eliminating the need for parallel expert loading or specialized hardware. Experiments show Omni-C achieves performance comparable to expert models in unimodal and cross-model tasks, with modest zero-shot degradation on audio and text that is largely recovered through lightweight linear probing or parameter efficient fine-tuning. The unified architecture substantially reduces inference memory usage compared to multi-encoder baselines, advancing efficient and scalable multimodal learning.

</details>
